# <a name="dimensions-and-measures-available-in-call-quality-dashboard"></a><span data-ttu-id="b913d-103">Dimensioni e misure disponibile nel Dashboard di qualità delle chiamate</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-103">Dimensions and measures available in Call Quality Dashboard</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b913d-104">La chiamata qualità Dashboard (CQD) per Microsoft Teams e Skype Business online consente di ottenere informazioni di base sulla qualità delle chiamate effettuate con Microsoft Teams e Skype per servizi di Business.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-104">The Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online allows you to gain insights into the quality of calls made using Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b913d-105">Questo argomento illustra nel dettaglio le dimensioni e metriche misurate dal CQD.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-105">This topic provides detailed information about the dimensions and measures exposed by CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b913d-106">Per ulteriori informazioni su CQD e come abilitarla, vedere [attivazione e l'utilizzo del Dashboard di qualità delle chiamate per team di Microsoft e Skype Business online](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-106">To learn more about CQD and how to enable it, see [Turning on and using Call Quality Dashboard for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>
  
## <a name="first-and-second-endpoint-classification"></a><span data-ttu-id="b913d-107">Classificazione del primo e secondo endpoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-107">First and Second endpoint classification</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b913d-p102">Molte delle dimensioni e misure del Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) sono classificate come prima o seconda. La seguente logica determina quale endpoint coinvolto nello stream o chiamata viene etichettato come primo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-p102">Many of the dimensions and measures in Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) are labeled as first or second. The following logic determines which endpoint involved in the stream or call is labeled as first:</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="b913d-110">Innanzitutto sarà sempre un endpoint del Server (MCU AV, Mediation Server, ecc.) se un Server interessato flusso/chiamata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-110">First will always be a Server endpoint (AV MCU, Mediation Server, etc.) if a Server is involved in the stream/call.</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="b913d-111">Il secondo endpoint sarà sempre un endpoint client a meno che lo stream non sia tra due endpoint server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-111">Second will always be a Client endpoint unless the stream is between two Server endpoints.</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="b913d-112">Se entrambi gli endpoint sono dello stesso tipo, l'ordine per il quale è il primo e secondo si basa sull'ordine interno della categoria di agente utente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-112">If both endpoints are the same type, the order for which is first vs. second is based on internal ordering of the user agent category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b913d-113">Ciò assicura che l'ordinamento sia coerente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-113">This ensures the ordering is consistent.</span></span>
    
<span data-ttu-id="b913d-114">Ad esempio, ciascuna riga rappresenta una coppia di agenti utente coinvolti in uno stream:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-114">For example, each row represents a pair of User Agents involved in a stream:</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="b913d-154">Questa classificazione primo-secondo è distinta da quale endpoint sia il chiamante o il chiamato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-154">That First and Second classification is separate from which endpoint is the caller or callee.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b913d-155">La dimensione primo chiamante è che può essere utilizzata per identificare punto finale che è stato il chiamante o il destinatario della chiamata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-155">The First Is Caller dimension which can be used to help identify which endpoint was the caller or callee.</span></span> 
  
## <a name="dimensions"></a><span data-ttu-id="b913d-156">Dimensioni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-156">Dimensions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b913d-157">La tabella seguente elenca le dimensioni attualmente disponibili in CQD.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-157">The following table lists the dimensions currently available in CQD:</span></span>

|:-----|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="b913d-158">**Nome della dimensione**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-158">**Dimension name**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="b913d-159">**Tipo di dati / Unità**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-159">**Data type / Units**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="b913d-160">**Descrizione**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-160">**Description**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="b913d-161">**Valori**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-161">**Values**</span></span> <br/> |

### <a name="notes-on-dimension-data-typeunits"></a><span data-ttu-id="b913d-1804">Note sul tipo di dati/unità delle dimensioni:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1804">Notes on dimension data type/units:</span></span>

#### <a name="range"></a><span data-ttu-id="b913d-1805">Intervallo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1805">Range</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1806">Le dimensioni fornite come intervallo o gruppo di valori sono indicate utilizzando il formato seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1806">Dimensions that are provided as range or group of values are shown using the following format:</span></span>
  
 <span data-ttu-id="b913d-1807">_<sort order string> [<lower bound inclusive> - <upper bound exclusive)_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1807">_<sort order string> [<lower bound inclusive> - <upper bound exclusive)_</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1808">Ad esempio, la dimensione Durata (Minuti) rappresenta la durata della chiamata in secondi e il valore è riferito come intervallo di valori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1808">For example, the Duration (Minutes) dimension represents the call duration in seconds with the value reported as a range of values.</span></span>

|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1809">**Duration (Minutes)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1809">**Duration (Minutes)**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1810">**Interpretazione**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1810">**How to interpret**</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1811">062: [0 - 0)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1811">062: [0 - 0)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1812">Durata flusso = 0 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1812">Stream duration = 0 minutes</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1813">064: [1 - 2)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1813">064: [1 - 2)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1814">1 minuto < = durata flusso < 2 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1814">1 minute < = stream duration < 2 minutes</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1815">065: [2 - 3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1815">065: [2 - 3)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1816">2 minuti < = durata flusso < 3 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1816">2 minutes < = stream duration < 3 minutes</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1817">066: [3 - 4)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1817">066: [3 - 4)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1818">3 minuti < = durata flusso < 4 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1818">3 minutes < = stream duration < 4 minutes</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1819">…</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1819"></span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1820">…</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1820"></span></span>  <br/> |
   
<span data-ttu-id="b913d-p272">La stringa <sort order string> si usa per controllare l'ordinamento quando si presentano i dati e si può utilizzare per filtrare. Ad esempio, un filtro su Durata (Minuti) < "065", mostrerà flussi con una durata inferiore a 2 minuti (lo "0" iniziale è necessario perché il filtro funzioni come previsto).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-p272">The <sort order string> is used to control the sort order when presenting the data and can be used for filtering. For example, a filter on Duration (Minutes) < "065", would show streams with duration less than 2 minutes (The leading '0' is needed for the filter to work as expected).</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="b913d-1823">Il valore effettivo della stringa di ordinamento non è significativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1823">The actual value of the sort order string isn't significant.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="enumeration-pair"></a><span data-ttu-id="b913d-1824">Coppia di enumerazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1824">Enumeration pair</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1825">Le dimensioni fornite come coppia di enumerazione sono indicate utilizzando il formato seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1825">Dimensions that are provided as an enumeration pair are shown using the following format:</span></span>
  
 <span data-ttu-id="b913d-1826">_<enumeration value from one end point> : < enumeration value from the other endpoint>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1826">_<enumeration value from one end point> : < enumeration value from the other endpoint>_</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1827">L'ordinamento dei valori di enumerazione è coerente ma non riflette l'ordinamento del primo e del secondo endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1827">The ordering of the enumeration values is consistent but doesn't reflect ordering of the first or second endpoints.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1828">Ad esempio, la coppia dettagli di connessione di rete mostra i valori dei dettagli di connessione di rete dei due endpoint:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1828">For example, the Network Connection Detail Pair shows the Network Connection Detail values for the two endpoints:</span></span>

|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1829">**Network Connection Detail Pair**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1829">**Network Connection Detail Pair**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1830">**Interpretazione**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1830">**How to interpret**</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1831">Cablata : Cablata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1831">Wired : Wired</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1832">Il primo e il secondo endpoint usavano entrambi connessioni ethernet cablate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1832">First and second endpoints both used wired ethernet connections.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1833">Cablata : WiFi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1833">Wired : wifi</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="b913d-1834">Il primo endpoint usava una connessione ethernet cablata mentre il secondo endpoint usava una connessione WiFi oppure il secondo endpoint usava una connessione ethernet cablata mentre il primo endpoint usava una connessione WiFi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1834">First endpoint used wired ethernet connection and second endpoint used Wi-Fi connection, or the second endpoint used wired ethernet connection and first endpoint used Wi-Fi connection.</span></span>  <br/> |

#### <a name="blank-values"></a><span data-ttu-id="b913d-1839">Valori vuoti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-1839">Blank values</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b913d-p273">Nella tabella sopra riportata sono elencati i motivi possibili per cui una dimensione potrebbe essere vuota. Molte dimensioni e misure sono vuote quando la dimensione disponibile nel record QoE (Quality of Experience) è falsa. In genere questa situazione si verifica quando non è stato possibile effettuare la chiamata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b913d-p273">The table above lists possible reasons why a dimension may be blank. Many dimensions and measures will be blank if the QoE Record Available dimension is false. This typically occurs when the call wasn't successfully established.</span></span>
